    1202 -    `Timer` is a non-visual component that fires events at regular intervals. It

    1219 -    1220 -‚Ä¢ Called xmlui.xmlui_component_docs({"component":"DataSource"})
    1221 -  ‚îî # DataSource [#datasource]
    1222 -
    1223 -    `DataSource` fetches and caches data from API endpoints, versus [`APICall`](/
          docs/reference/components/APICall) which
    1224 -        creates, updates or deletes data.
    1225 -
    1226 -    **Key characteristics:**    1227 [38;5;1;48;5;52m-    - **Conditional loading**: Use `when` property to prevent fetching until depe
          ndent data is ready    - **Built-in caching**: Prevents unnecessary requests and
          provides instant data access
    1228 -    - **Polling support**: Automatically refetch data at specified intervals
    1229 -    - **Data transformation**: Process and filter responses before components use
           the data

    434 -        enabled or disabled and ensures that the timer event handler completes bef
         ore

    436 -
    437 -    The following sample demonstrates many aspects of the `Timer` component. Use t         he[49m

    440 -    ```xmlui-pg display copy name="Using Timer"
    441 -    <App ...
    442 -
    443 -‚Ä¢ Called xmlui.xmlui_component_docs({"component":"DataSource"})
    444 -  ‚îî # DataSource [#datasource]    445 -
    446 -    `DataSource` fetches and caches data from API endpoints, versus [`APICall`](/d
         ocs/
    447 -        reference/components/APICall) which creates, updates or deletes data.
    448 -
